original text:  // Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Use a clocked always block
    //   copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
    //   Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments
    
    always @(posedge clk)
        q <= d;

endmodule

// Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Create a clocked always block
    //   copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
    //   Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments
    
    always @(posedge clk)
        q <= d;

endmodule

// Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Use a clocked always block
    //   copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
    //   Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments
    
    always @(posedge clk)
        q <= d;

endmodule

// Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Use a clocked always block

        q <= d;

// Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Create a clocked always block
    //   copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
    //   Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments
    
    always @(posedge clk)
        q <= d;

endmodule

// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );

// Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Use a clocked always block
    //   copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
    always @(posedge clk)
        q <= d;

// Create a single D flip-flop.
// Use a clocked always block
// copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
// Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments

module top_module (
    input clk,    // Clocks are used in sequential circuits
    input d,
    output reg q );
    
    // Use a clocked always block
    //   copy d to q at every positive edge of clk
    //   Clocked always blocks should use non-blocking assignments
    
    always @(posedge clk)
        q <= d;
